</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Provides Update on Long-Term Growth Strategy at 2022 Investor Day </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Confirms strong long-term growth prospects and competitive advantages as a global snacking leader
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unveils evolution of long-term strategy to accelerate growth and focus portfolio on attractive chocolate,
biscuits and baked snacks categories </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Updates long-term algorithm to 3% - 5% Organic Net Revenue growth, up from 3%+ </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Continues portfolio reshaping to accelerate growth and focus </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CHICAGO, May</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;10, 2022 &#150;</B> Mondel&#275;z International (Nasdaq: MDLZ) today unveiled the evolution of its strategy to accelerate
growth and focus its portfolio to generate strong, sustainable shareholder value. As a result, the Company is updating its long-term algorithm to 3% - 5% Organic Net Revenue growth, up from previous guidance of 3% plus. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our competitive advantages in the marketplace and focused strategy on global snacking leadership give us great confidence in our ability to sustain
strong <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-</FONT> and bottom-line growth for many years to come,&#148; said Dirk Van de Put, Chairman&nbsp;&amp; Chief Executive Officer, Mondel&#275;z International. &#147;Building on our category leadership,
favorable geographic footprint, and the power of our iconic brands, we are well positioned for stronger growth in the decade ahead.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company
will continue to prioritize <I>Growth, Execution</I> and <I>Culture </I>as three pillars of its strategy &#150; investing in differentiated marketing and sales capabilities, while strengthening its local-first operating model to further empower
employees and promote a growth culture. Recognizing the urgent challenges facing the planet and the communities in which it operates, the Company also is elevating <I>Sustainability </I>to become a fourth pillar in its long-term growth strategy. By
further advancing its <I>Snacking Made Right</I> agenda across a focused set of environmental, social and governance priorities, Mondel&#275;z International aims to help drive positive change at scale &#150; creating long-term value for both the
business and its stakeholders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Accelerated Growth and Portfolio Focus </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International is reshaping its portfolio, with a long-term vision to accelerate growth and generate 90% of revenue in chocolate and biscuits,
including baked snacks. Chocolate and biscuits are attractive and historically durable categories in both developed and emerging markets, with significant headroom to increase penetration and per capita consumption. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company will strengthen its presence in its core categories in major markets by building on existing distribution, expanding in high-growth channels and
leveraging its iconic brands to establish multi-category leadership positions. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As it continues to reshape its portfolio, Mondel&#275;z International will drive value through organic
growth and targeted acquisitions that expand its presence in chocolate, biscuits and baked snacks by filling geographic gaps and extending into under-represented segments and price tiers. The eight acquisitions Mondel&#275;z International has
completed or announced since 2018 add $2&nbsp;billion in annual revenue, and have had an average growth rate in the high single digits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Additionally, the
Company announced plans to divest its developed market gum business after completing a strategic review over the past year. The Company also disclosed its intention to divest the global <I>Halls</I> business. Mondel&#275;z International will
continue to operate other brands and products within its candy business, as well as its emerging market gum business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Investing in Capabilities and
Culture </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To enable its refined growth strategy, Mondel&#275;z International announced significant investments in capabilities and culture &#150;
including investing more than $1&nbsp;billion to become the digital commerce snacks leader. The Company aims to deliver 20% of revenues from digital channels by 2030, up from 6% of 2021 revenues. Along with its investments in technology, the Company
is investing behind future-forward commercial growth capabilities &#150; including integrated agile processes to drive simpler ways of working; expanded commercial excellence training programs; and increased digital learning opportunities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our growth ambition will not be possible without the passion, dedication and commitment of our people &#150; the very best in the consumer packaged
goods industry,&#148; Van de Put said. &#147;To accelerate our growth and focus, we are taking our talent and culture strategy to the next level &#150; by doubling down on initiatives to advance diversity, equity and inclusion; expanding investment
in top talent programs; and rolling out a global, holistic employee well-being program.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Updating Long Term Growth Algorithm </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International is updating its long-term growth algorithm to 3% - 5% Organic Net Revenue growth, up from 3% plus previously, to reflect the
evolution of the strategy. The Company continues to expect Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis in the high single digits and gradually increasing Free Cash Flow of $3&nbsp;billion plus over the long term. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is confident it can accelerate and sustain profitable growth and achieve this refined long-term algorithm as a result of: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Consistent delivery against our financial commitments, investment in the long-term health of our brands and the capabilities of our people &#150;
combined with our key competitive advantages &#150; position us well to create significant value for our stakeholders,&#148; said Luca Zaramella, Mondel&#275;z International&#146;s Chief Financial Officer. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Webcast and Materials </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The investor update presentation and presentation slides will be available in the investors section of the Company&#146;s website
(<U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U>), and a recording of the event will also be available on the website after the presentation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z
International </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2021 net
revenues of approximately $29&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>Oreo, belVita</I> and <I>LU</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk, Milka </I>and <I>Toblerone </I>chocolate; <I>Sour
Patch Kids</I> candy and <I>Trident </I>gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit www.mondelezinternational.com or follow the Company on Twitter at
<U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>End Note </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Organic Net
